- **Behavior change (B1 review nit A):** because the pickup-source gate lives in the SHARED `OriginHasCargo`, an already-shipped M3a SINGLE-window pickup route is now ALSO pickup-source-gated at dispatch (previously the pickup side debited at the dock crossing UNGATED; the docked-origin gate did not cover the pickup endpoint). This is correct-by-design (gate-before-debit, scenario 5.2/5.3 - a pickup route should hold when its source is dry rather than debit nothing), but it is a genuine behavior change for M3a pickup routes, not a byte no-op. Carried to B4: an in-game regression that an M3a pickup route still DISPATCHES when its source is stocked (and HOLDS naming the source when dry).
- **Tests.** `RoutePickupSourceGateTests.cs` (NEW, pure xUnit, hand-rolled resolver + per-vessel readers): `TwoSources_BothCover_Eligible`, `TwoSources_AShort_HoldsNamingSourceA`, `TwoSources_BShort_HoldsNamingSourceB`, `TwoSources_BothShort_FirstShortByDockUT_NamesEarliest` (stops presented in reverse UT order still name the dock-UT-earliest short - the deterministic first-short ordering), `SamePid_TwoWindows_SumAgainstOneTank_Short` + `SamePid_TwoWindows_CollapseToOneGroup` (the under-gate guard: two windows on one pid SUM, do not each see the full tank), `DockedOriginPlusPickupSource_DoNotDoubleCount` (a delivery stop is not a source; the origin `CostManifest` does not leak into the pickup gate), `DeliveryOnly_NoPickupSources_ZeroGroups_Eligible` (byte-behaviour identity for a delivery-only / single-origin route), `NullAndEmptyStops_PassTrivially`, `PickupSourceUnresolved_HoldsWithReason`, `InventoryPickupSource_Short_HoldsNamingSource`, `SamePid_InventoryWindows_Sum`. `LogisticsHoldPresentationTests.cs` gained `DescribeHold_PickupSourceShort_NamesSourceVesselAndResource`, `DescribeHold_PickupSourceInventoryShort_NamesSource`, `DescribeHold_PickupSourceUnresolved`, `DescribeHold_PickupSourceShort_UnnamedSource`, plus the new tokens added to the plain-ASCII guard. Full xUnit suite green at 15921 (up from the M4a A5 baseline 15905). The ERS/ELS grep gate passes (the new gate reads no `RecordingStore.CommittedRecordings` / `Ledger.Actions`).
- **Pending (later phases):** ~~escrow map + lifecycle clear/drop + `ResetForTesting` (B2)~~ DONE in B2 (see the B2 section below); ~~per-window source debit firing under the windowed replay key + lift the M4a >1-source-window defer (B3)~~ DONE in B3 (see the B3 section below); in-game `LogisticsMultiOriginRuntimeTests` + synthetic multi-origin recording + design-doc 19.4 M4 multi-origin bullet flip (B4).

### Logistics M4b Phase B2 - RAM-only cargo escrow map + lifecycle + B1 gate net (done, branch `logistics-m4-multistop`)

Plan `docs/dev/plan-logistics-m4-shape-generality.md` Phase B2 (D11, OQ7: RAM-only `RouteStore` escrow, DROP-not-revert, the four clear sites, net into the B1 source gate). B2 builds the MAP + NET + LIFECYCLE only; NOTHING reserves yet (the reserve-at-dispatch / release-at-window-debit firing is B3), so in production the escrow is always empty and the net is a no-op (byte-behaviour-identical to B1). No user-facing CHANGELOG line yet (B3 makes it functional); the design-doc 19.4 M4 multi-origin bullet is NOT yet flipped.

- **`RouteStore` RAM-only escrow map.** `private static readonly Dictionary<string, Dictionary<uint, Dictionary<string, double>>> cargoEscrow` keyed `routeId -> vesselPid -> resourceName -> reserved amount` (a per-RESOURCE sub-map per `(routeId, pid)` so a depot can reserve LiquidFuel + Oxidizer against one source independently). NOT serialized: `SaveRoutesTo` / `LoadRoutesFrom` never touch it. Pure RAM - holds nothing from the committed-recording set or the ledger action list, so it passes the ERS/ELS grep gate (`scripts/grep-audit-ers-els.ps1` via `GrepAuditTests`) with NO allowlist entry (the doc comment was worded to avoid the literal `\.CommittedRecordings` / `\bLedger\.Actions\b` grep patterns).
- **Methods.** `ReserveCargo(routeId, pid, resource, amount)` (accumulate; non-positive / null-key ignored), `ReleaseCargo(routeId, pid, resource, amount)` (subtract, clamp at zero, prune empty resource/pid/route entries), `DropRouteEscrow(routeId)` (drop a route's WHOLE reservation - tombstone / remove / abort), `ClearAllEscrow(reason)` (lifecycle clear), `OtherRoutesReservedFor(forRouteId, pid, resource)` (the NET read - sums reservations held by every OTHER route on that pid+resource), plus `GetReservedForTesting` / `EscrowRouteCountForTesting` diagnostics. Reserve / Release / Drop / Clear log `(routeId, pid, resource, amount, new-total)` (DropRouteEscrow / ClearAllEscrow log a single batch summary).
- **NET semantics (the crux - subtract OTHER routes, not this route's own).** `available_for_R = live_stored(pid, resource) - sum(cargoEscrow[r][pid][resource] for r != R)`. A route does NOT subtract its OWN reservation (it owns what it reserved). This is the competing-route protection: route A reserves 100 from depot X at dispatch; route B gating X in the same / a later tick (before A's physical debit) sees X's available reduced by A's 100 and cannot double-claim it. Wired at the B1 seam in `LiveRouteRuntimeEnvironment.PickupSourcesHaveCargo` - the `Resolver` wraps `probe.ProbeResourceStored` as `name => max(0, live(name) - RouteStore.OtherRoutesReservedFor(routeId, sourcePid, name))`. Pure-RAM subtraction; no-op until something reserves (B3). The grouping / summing / first-short logic in `RoutePickupSourceGate` is unchanged.
- **Four clear sites (OQ7).** (1) `onGameSceneSwitchRequested` (any within-game scene change) - new `ParsekScenario.OnGameSceneSwitchClearEscrow(FromToAction)` subscribed idempotently in `SubscribeVesselLifecycleEvents` (Remove-then-Add, called from OnLoad) + removed in `OnDestroy`; the in-cycle reservation is recomputed from pending route state next tick, so it need not survive a scene change. (2) `ParsekScenario.OnMainMenuTransition` (game unload) - mirrors the existing RAM-cache resets there (`PlaybackScopeTracker.Reset` etc.), NOT `OnLoad` (which runs every scene-enter and would wrongly clear a mid-cycle reservation). (3) `RouteStore.RemoveRoute` - a removed / tombstoned route drops its escrow key via `DropRouteEscrow` (belt-and-suspenders; hooks RemoveRoute, NOT SupersedeCommit, since a reservation is reserve-and-released within one EmitLoopCycle). (4) `ResetForTesting` - clears the escrow alongside the routes (else `[Collection("Sequential")]` tests leak). DROP-not-revert: escrow has no ledger row; the physical debit's revert is the rewind quicksave + ELS replay keys (RouteModule observe-only).
- **Inventory escrow: SEAM for B3, not done.** The resource escrow is the primary deliverable (plan D11). The inventory counter passes through the resolver unmodified; the symmetric inventory-escrow analogue (keyed by IdentityHash) is one analogous wrap away and is deferred to B3 per D11 ("inventory escrow only if a multi-window inventory consolidation opens the gap").
- **Tests.** `RouteCargoEscrowTests.cs` (NEW, `[Collection("Sequential")]` + ResetForTesting): `Reserve_OtherRouteSeesLess_OwnerExcludesOwn` (A reserves -> B sees less, A excludes its own - the headline net), `Reserve_NetIsPerResourceAndPerPid` (no leak across resource/pid), `TwoRoutesReserve_ThirdSeesBoth_ReleaseRaisesAvailable` (sums ALL other routes; release one raises availability), `Release_PartialThenOverRelease_ClampsAtZero` (partial + over-release clamp, no negative residual), `Reserve_Accumulates` (second reserve sums - OQ6), `DropRouteEscrow_RemovesAllOfARoute_RaisesCompetitorAvailable` (drops all pids of A, competitor restored, B untouched), `RemoveRoute_DropsItsEscrow` (RemoveRoute drops the key), `ClearAllEscrow_EmptiesEveryRoute` (lifecycle clear), `ResetForTesting_ClearsEscrow_NoLeak` (sequential-collection leak guard), `Escrow_IsNotSerialized_RoundTripLeavesItUntouched` (SaveRoutesTo / LoadRoutesFrom never persist or reload escrow; a clean-RAM load yields zero escrow), `CompetingRoute_HeldByReservation_ThroughRealGate` (the competing-route case END-TO-END through the real `RoutePickupSourceGate.Evaluate` with the production net wrap: A reserves 300 of depot X's 400 LF -> B's 200 LF pickup HELD naming depot X; A releases -> B covers), `NoReservation_NetIsNoOp` (the net is byte-behaviour-identical to B1 when nothing is reserved). Full xUnit suite green at 15933 (up from the B1 baseline 15921). The ERS/ELS grep gate passes (the escrow reads no committed-recording set / ledger action list).
- **Pending (later phases):** ~~per-window source debit firing - reserve at dispatch + release at each window phase under the windowed replay key + lift the M4a >1-source-window defer + the inventory-escrow analogue if the gap opens (B3)~~ DONE in B3 (see the B3 section below); in-game `LogisticsMultiOriginRuntimeTests` + synthetic multi-origin recording + design-doc 19.4 M4 multi-origin bullet flip (B4).

### Logistics M4b Phase B3 - per-window source-debit firing + reserve/debit/release escrow lifecycle (done, branch `logistics-m4-multistop`)

Plan `docs/dev/plan-logistics-m4-shape-generality.md` Phase B3 (D5 reuse, D10, D11/OQ7: the firing + escrow lifecycle - the M4b correctness keystone, same high-risk loop-route firing transaction as the M4a A3 blocker). B3 LIFTS the M4a multi-pickup defer and wires the reserve-at-dispatch / release-at-each-window-debit ESCROW lifecycle onto the per-window firing. NO user-facing CHANGELOG line yet (B4 closes M4b end-to-end + validates in-game); the design-doc 19.4 M4 multi-origin bullet is NOT yet flipped.

- **Defer-lift (the M4a multi-pickup defer was a STALE COMMENT, not a code gate).** Investigation confirmed `RouteOrchestrator.EmitMultiStopWindow` ALREADY called `EmitPickupHalf` per due window in M4a A3, with `PendingStopIndex` driven to that window's stop index (so `ResolveCycleStop` resolves THAT stop's `PickupManifest`) and the C-2 `IsPickupAlreadyInLedger((RouteId, cycleId, stopIndex))` backstop already keyed per-window. So the >1 source-debiting multi-window firing was mechanically already in place - the ">1 source-debiting pickup window is M4b territory" line was only a comment. B3 rewrote that comment to describe the lifted behaviour (each window's source debit fires at its own dock phase, idempotent per window across reload; the single bidirectional M3a window is byte-behaviour-identical). The single-window M3a pickup path is unchanged.
- **RESERVE at dispatch (the escrow crux).** New `RouteOrchestrator.ReserveCycleEscrow(route, ut, env, cycleId)` called ONCE per cycle at dispatch (post-eligibility, pre-emit) in BOTH firing paths: the multi-stop `ProcessMultiStopCrossings` eligible-first-commit branch (right after `EmitDispatchDebit`) and the single-stop `EmitLoopCycle` (right after its `EmitDispatchDebit`). It builds the per-pid SUMMED reservation list from the route's pickup `Stops` via the NEW pure `RoutePickupSourceGate.TryBuildReservations` (reuses `TryBuildSourceGroups` - the SAME grouping the B1 gate uses), then calls `RouteStore.ReserveCargo(routeId, resolvedPid, resource, summedAmount)` once per (pid, resource). **Keyed on the SAME resolved pid the B1 gate nets on:** `ResolveEscrowSourcePid` resolves the live vessel via `env.TryResolveEndpointVessel` and returns `vessel.persistentId` (exactly what `ApplyPickupDebit`'s `OriginVesselPid` carries), falling back to the endpoint's craft-baked `VesselPersistentId` when the env returns no live vessel (headless / off-Unity). On an unresolved pickup source the build returns false and NOTHING is reserved (a partial reservation set would leak; the eligibility gate normally held the cycle first).
- **DEBIT + RELEASE at each window phase.** New `RouteOrchestrator.ReleaseWindowEscrow(route, stop, resolvedPid, cycleId, context)` called inside `EmitPickupHalf` AFTER `ApplyPickupDebit` returns, releasing THIS window's OWN `PickupManifest` amounts against the pid the debit resolved (`pickup.OriginVesselPid`). After the cycle's LAST pickup window releases, the source's SUMMED reservation nets to exactly zero (reserve == sum-of-per-window-releases per pid). The debit is NOT gated on transport disposition (19.2.5: a crashed transport still debits the witnessed source), so the release follows the debit unconditionally on the resolved path.
- **Release on window-skip / endpoint-lost (no leak); drop on abort.** When a pickup window's endpoint is LOST mid-cycle (OQ4: `ApplyPickupDebit` returns `Unresolved=true`, zero actuals, cargo NOT taken), `EmitPickupHalf` still RELEASEs the window's reservation - keyed on the escrow-resolve pid (the debit outcome carries pid 0 when unresolved) - so the hold is freed without debiting (warn + skip + continue, NOT abort: the cycle still completes and surviving windows still fire). A blocked cycle never reserved (reserve is post-eligibility); the B2 lifecycle clears (`onGameSceneSwitchRequested` -> `ClearAllEscrow`, `RouteStore.RemoveRoute` -> `DropRouteEscrow`, `OnMainMenuTransition`, `ResetForTesting`) are the BACKSTOP for any orphaned hold.
- **Leak-free invariant (stated + tested).** EVERY Reserve is matched by a Release within the cycle (a physical debit OR a window endpoint-lost skip), OR a Drop on tombstone / scene-change / cycle-complete. Reserve fires once per cycle (the per-pid summed amount); each pickup window releases its own portion at its debit phase, so the route's escrow nets to zero by cycle end - asserted via `RouteStore.EscrowRouteCountForTesting == 0` after each cycle completes. A PARTIAL cycle (window A fires this tick, window B next tick) keeps window B's source reservation LIVE across the gap (a competing route's B1 gate sees it).
- **C1 - re-establish from PENDING windows on a `dispatchAlready` resume (honors OQ7/D11 "recomputed from pending state on the next Tick").** The escrow is RAM-only / not persisted, so a within-game scene switch (`onGameSceneSwitchRequested` -> `ClearAllEscrow`) or a reload that lands MID-cycle drops the un-fired window's hold; the cycle then resumes with `dispatchAlready=true`, so the dispatch-time `ReserveCycleEscrow` does NOT re-run and the hold would be silently lost - a competing route could drain the source in the gap (violating 19.2.5 strand-protection). FIX: `ProcessMultiStopCrossings`' dispatchAlready resume branch calls `ReEstablishEscrowForUnfiredWindows(route, ut, env, cycleId, cMin)`, which re-reserves ONLY the cycle's still-UN-FIRED pickup windows (`stop.LastFiredCycleIndex < cMin`; a window already debited+released this cycle has its hold consumed and is NOT re-reserved). It uses a new `RoutePickupSourceGate.TryBuildReservations` overload taking a `Func<RouteStop,bool>` un-fired filter (forwarded to a filtered `TryBuildSourceGroups`). **IDEMPOTENT:** it runs ONLY when the route currently holds NO escrow (new `RouteStore.HasEscrow(routeId)` accessor) - a normal in-session resume (no clear happened) still holds its reservation, so it short-circuits and does NOT double-reserve. The single-stop `EmitLoopCycle` path is UNTOUCHED (its `IsDispatchAlreadyInLedger` early-return precedes the reserve; reserve==release within one tick, no gap).
- **C2 - cycle-complete drop-residual sweep (closes the reserve-pid != release-pid leak robustly).** At cycle-complete (the `cycleLastDockReached` once-per-cycle bump site) `ProcessMultiStopCrossings` calls `RouteStore.DropRouteEscrow(route.Id)`. Rationale: at cycle-complete every window has fired (or been skipped), so any remaining reservation is stale - e.g. a window whose resolved release pid diverged from the dispatch-time reserve pid (a mid-cycle source-identity change / surface-fallback / craft-baked-pid regeneration), where the release missed the reserved key. Dropping the whole route's escrow guarantees no positive-residual leak regardless of pid divergence. Safe because loop routes are single-instance (cadence >= span, only one cycle in flight). This also drops C1's re-established reservation when the cycle finishes. A no-op when nothing is held (the normal leak-free path already netted to zero).
- **Inventory escrow: DECISION - resource escrow suffices, inventory escrow NOT wired.** Per plan D11 ("inventory escrow only if a multi-window inventory consolidation opens the gap"), the resource escrow is the primary deliverable. The inventory pickup half (`ApplyInventoryPickupDebit`) is window-local and the inventory counter passes through `RoutePickupSourceGate` unmodified; `TryBuildReservations` builds NO reservation for an inventory-only pickup window. The symmetric inventory-escrow analogue (keyed by `IdentityHash`) stays the deferred B3 seam, one analogous wrap away. RATIONALE: the gameplay scenarios that motivate escrow (families 3/6: refinery/depot resource consolidation) are resource flows; no shipped scenario opens a multi-window inventory consolidation with a dispatch-to-debit gap.
- **Cross-cycle correctness.** The A3 one-dock-cycle-per-pass `cMin` catch-up + cycleId-uniqueness holds for the source-debit windows: each fired cycle reserves once (its own cycleId), debits each window once, and releases each window once, so reservations do not leak across the cross-cycle catch-up. Pinned by `CrossCycleGapTick_MultiPickup_EachSourceDebitsOncePerCycle_NoLeak` (two complete cycles -> each source debited exactly twice, escrow empty).
- **Tests.** Pure: `RoutePickupSourceGateTests` (NEW B3 cases) - `Reservations_KeyOnResolvedPid_SumSamePidWindows` (one entry per resolved pid, same-pid windows SUM), `Reservations_InventoryOnlyAndDeliveryOnly_ReserveNothing` (inventory-only / delivery-only reserve nothing), `Reservations_UnresolvedSource_ReturnsFalse_NoPartialSet` (unresolved short-circuits the build), `Reservations_UnfiredWindowFilter_ExcludesAlreadyFiredWindow` (C1: the un-fired filter excludes an already-fired window from the rebuild). Real-path (NEW `RouteEscrowFireTests.cs`, `[Collection("Sequential")]`, through the production `RouteOrchestrator.Tick` -> `ProcessMultiStopCrossings` / `EmitPickupHalf` with the A3 `PickupDebitApplierForTesting` + `DeliveryRowEmitterForTesting` seams): `TwoSourceRun_BothSourceDebitsFire_EscrowEmptyAfterCycle_NoLeak` (both source debits at their windows + escrow empty after), `Shuttle_DebitsRefineryAtItsWindow_EscrowEmptyAfterCycle` (refinery debited at its window), `PartialCycle_UnfiredWindowReservationLive_CompetingRouteSeesIt` (partial-cycle hold stays live; competing route's net sees it), `WindowEndpointLost_ReleasesReservation_CycleStillCompletes` (endpoint-lost releases + cycle continues), `CrashedDisposition_StillDebitsSource` (debit not disposition-gated), `CrossCycleGapTick_MultiPickup_EachSourceDebitsOncePerCycle_NoLeak`, `IdempotentAcrossReload_NoDoubleDebit` (C-2 backstop, no double-debit), `SingleWindowM3aPickup_BehaviourIdentical_EscrowNetsZeroInTick` (no M3a regression), `DeliveryOnlyRoute_ReservesNothing`, `DispatchAlreadyResumeAfterClear_ReestablishesUnfiredWindowReservation` (C1: a mid-cycle clear then resume re-establishes the un-fired window's hold; a competing route sees it again), `DispatchAlreadyResumeNoClear_DoesNotDoubleReserve` (C1 idempotency: a normal in-session resume does NOT re-reserve), `CycleComplete_DropsResidual_WhenReleasePidDiverges` (C2: a reserve-pid != release-pid divergence's residual is swept at cycle-complete). Full xUnit suite green at 15949 (the C1/C2 fold added +4 over the B3-commit baseline 15945).
- ~~**Pending (later phase):** in-game `LogisticsMultiOriginRuntimeTests` (shuttle + A+B consolidation, escrow competing-hold, SaveGame round-trip) + synthetic multi-origin recording + the user-facing CHANGELOG line + design-doc 19.4 M4 multi-origin bullet flip + 19.3 scenario-family rows 3/6 + 19.2.5 flip (B4).~~ DONE in B4 (below).

### Logistics M4b Phase B4 - in-game validation + M4b docs close (done, branch `logistics-m4-multistop`)

Plan `docs/dev/plan-logistics-m4-shape-generality.md` Phase B4: closes M4b end-to-end with in-game tests + a synthetic recording + the user-facing CHANGELOG line + the design-doc flips. NO production-code change (the B1/B2/B3 firing path is complete); this phase is tests + docs only. Round-trip linking stays M4c (NOT shipped) - the CHANGELOG line does not overclaim it.

- **In-game `LogisticsMultiOriginRuntimeTests`** (new `Source/Parsek/InGameTests/`, `[InGameTest(Category="Logistics", Scene=FLIGHT, AllowBatchExecution=false, RestoreBatchFlightBaselineAfterExecution=true)]`, isolated-batch + `WaitForActiveVesselUnpack` discipline). Six tests; live validation (Ctrl+Shift+T) is the maintainer's playtest, the M1/M2/M3/M4a pattern. (1) `MultiOrigin_TwoSources_BothDebitedAndConsolidated` (5.3): a route with two auto-spawned depot sources + a delivery; both depots' LiquidFuel drop by their window manifests through the production `Tick` -> `ProcessMultiStopCrossings` -> `EmitPickupHalf` -> `ApplyPickupDebit` path, two `RouteCargoPickedUp` rows (distinct stop indices), `CompletedCycles==1`. (2) `MultiOrigin_OneSourceShort_HoldsNamingSource`: depot B drained dry -> the WHOLE cycle holds all-or-nothing, depot A NOT debited (cycle never committed), `SkippedCycles>=1`, the hold token (`LastHoldDetail`) names the short source via the `source:<pid>` token. (3) `Shuttle_RefineryLoadThenStationDeliver_DebitsRefinery` (5.2): a 2-window non-KSC route loads from an auto-spawned refinery at its window then delivers at the station; the refinery LiquidFuel drops by the loaded amount, one pickup + one delivery row. (4) `Escrow_CompetingRouteSeesReservation_Holds`: route A `RouteStore.ReserveCargo`s a shared auto-spawned source at dispatch; route B's live `LiveRouteRuntimeEnvironment.OriginHasCargo` gate (B was eligible before) HOLDS after, the net via `OtherRoutesReservedFor`, naming the source. (5) `MultiOrigin_SaveRoundTrip_ResumesAndReEstablishesEscrow`: tick to depot A only, a real `GamePersistence.SaveGame` persists the partial fire state (stop 0 fired, stops 1+ unfired) into the `.sfs`, reload via the production `RouteStore.LoadRoutesFrom` codec, then tick to depot B + the station completes the SAME cycle once (depot A not re-debited; escrow is RAM-only + re-establishes on the resume; nets to zero / `HasEscrow` false after). (6) `M3aSingleWindowPickup_NotRegressedByNewGate` (B1-review nit A regression): a single-window pickup route PASSES the live source gate when stocked and HOLDS naming the source when dry - the M3a pickup path is a special case of the new N-source gate, not regressed.
- **Source provisioning + seams.** The consolidation depots, the shuttle refinery, and the shared escrow source are auto-spawned via `UnloadedFuelVesselFixture.EnsureUnloadedLiquidFuelVessel` (a fresh-identity pad-rocket copy in a parking orbit; reuses an existing suitable unloaded vessel when present), torn down in finally. The Tick-driven cases (1/2/3/5) run the REAL `ApplyPickupDebit` / `ApplyDelivery` production path against live source vessels (NO `PickupDebitApplierForTesting` / `DeliveryRowEmitterForTesting` seam - those B3 seams are the xUnit headless path; in-game uses the real debit). The escrow-hold (4) + the M3a-regression (6) drive the pure `LiveRouteRuntimeEnvironment.OriginHasCargo` gate directly (no Tick, single-stop routes), reusing the active vessel as the source. A precondition that can't be met (auto-spawn fails, save layout mismatch) calls `InGameAssert.Skip` with a named reason - never a hard fail.
- **Synthetic multi-origin recording.** New `SyntheticRecordingTests.MultiOriginConsolidationRouteTree`, wired into `InjectAllRecordings`: a transport launches, loads 100 Ore at Depot A (pickup window), undocks, loads 200 Ore at Depot B, undocks, delivers the consolidated 300 Ore at the station (the LAST dock), undocks. Two PICKUP windows (sign-flip of delivery: endpoint loses, transport gains) + one delivery window; flow closes (launched 0 + loaded 300 - delivered 300 - residual 0 = 0). Modeled on `MultiStopDeliveryRouteTree` (run manifests on every active-stop leg; a tail the route render end-trims away). `InjectAllRecordings` may env-flake on a shared-install IOException - not a code regression; re-run.
- **CHANGELOG.** One `## Unreleased` Features line scoped PRECISELY to what M4b shipped: multi-origin (load from several depots + consolidate; the shuttle load-then-deliver), all-or-nothing source gating (waits naming the short depot), cargo escrow (a competing route can't drain a shared depot mid-run). Does NOT overclaim round-trip (M4c, not shipped).
- **Design-doc flips.** 19.4 M4 multi-origin bullet -> SHIPPED (M4b) with the as-built note (sources derived from pickup stops - no new Route field; all-or-nothing N-source gate via `RoutePickupSourceGate` first-short names the source; RAM-only `RouteStore` escrow reserve-at-dispatch / debit-at-window / release + re-establish-on-resume + cycle-complete drop + scene-change/unload/removal clear; per-window source debit under the windowed replay key; inventory escrow deferred window-local). 19.2.5 - both locked semantics marked IMPLEMENTED (M4b). 19.3 row 6 (multi-origin) + row 3 (the shuttle) SHIPPED in M4b. 19.7 item 6 (escrow host) marked SHIPPED. Round-trip stays NEEDS M4c. Missions locked-layer git diff stays EMPTY.
- **Verification.** `dotnet test` green at 15949 (B4 is tests-via-`InGameTest` + a synthetic recording fixture + docs, so no xUnit count change). The Parsek project compiles (the in-game tests build via the Tests-project ProjectReference). LIVE validation (Ctrl+Shift+T) PENDING - the maintainer's playtest.
- **B4 follow-up: multi-origin fixture provisioning (test-infra, after the first playtest skipped the 4 multi-source tests).** The first playtest skipped tests (1)/(2)/(4)/(5): two issues, both in the test fixture (NOT the B1/B2/B3 production firing path). (a) Same-pid depots: the two consolidation depots both called `UnloadedFuelVesselFixture.EnsureUnloadedLiquidFuelVessel`, and the step-a reuse fast-path (`TryFindExistingUnloadedVessel`) handed the second call the just-spawned depot A (now itself an existing unloaded vessel) - depot A and depot B resolved to the SAME pid, so the two-source gate skipped. Fix: added an `excludeReusePids` parameter (pure `IsReuseExcluded` predicate); the second provisioning call passes depot A's resolved pid so the reuse path skips it and spawns a fresh, distinct-pid depot (`preserveIdentity:false` mints a new identity on every spawn). The single-source tests pass no exclude set (default null) - reuse behavior unchanged. (b) Too-big escrow source: `Escrow_CompetingRouteSeesReservation_Holds` spawned a source carrying the donor pad rocket's full tank (>= 2x the pickup), so a competing route could cover both and the reservation hold could not be demonstrated. Fix: added a `capStoredLf` cap to `AdjustSnapshotLiquidFuel` that clamps the spawned tank's stored amount EXACTLY (max = cap + free, donor's large capacity NOT preserved); the escrow test caps the shared source to `PickupAmountA + epsilon` (< 2x). Both depots are cleaned up in finally (two `Cleanup(...)` calls). Pure xUnit coverage added in `UnloadedFuelVesselFixtureTests` (cap clamp + override + bound-below-2x; `IsReuseExcluded` null/empty/in-set/other-pid). The `InGameAssert.Skip` fallback stays for a genuine spawn failure. Live re-validation PENDING.

### Logistics M4c Phase C1 - round-trip linking chain-constraint scheduler (done, branch `logistics-m4-multistop`)

Plan `docs/dev/plan-logistics-m4-shape-generality.md` Phase C1 (D12 / OQ8): the thin `LinkedRouteId` chain-constraint scheduler. Route B (linked to A) holds until A completes a cycle, alternating A->B->A. C2 (in-game validation + M4c docs close + the user-facing CHANGELOG line + the 19.4 round-trip + section 9 design flips) is the follow-up; this phase ships production code + xUnit + the dev entry only (NO user-facing CHANGELOG line yet, the 19.4 round-trip bullet stays NEEDS M4c).

- **New `RouteDispatchEvaluator.EligibilityFailureKind.WaitingForPartner`** (an evaluator enum value, appended LAST; NOT a `RouteStatus`, so the three `RouteStatusPolicy` throw-on-default switches are untouched and a waiting route stays `Active` / `GhostDriving` / renders its loop). Mapped in `EvaluateRoute` to a plain `Skip` (the legacy self-timer path is dead for loop routes, and the chain constraint is not a route STATUS so there is no `Wait*` decision for it); the live consumer is the loop-clock path.
- **Partner gate in `CheckEligibility`, ORDERED LAST** (gate 9, after ERS / endpoint / origin-cargo / funds / destination-capacity), so a genuinely-blocked route surfaces its REAL blocker first and the partner wait is the lowest-priority hold. The gate (`PartnerConstraintSatisfied`): an unlinked route (`LinkedRouteId == null`) returns true with NO RouteStore read (byte-behaviour-identical); a linked route resolves the partner via **`RouteStore.TryGetRoute`** (a static, the same seam M4b used to read escrow - NO new `IRouteRuntimeEnvironment` member, so the ~14 env fakes are UNTOUCHED, plan RANK-10; RouteStore reads committedRoutes only, NOT ERS/ELS, so no audit-gate concern); holds `WaitingForPartner` when `partner.CompletedCycles <= route.LastConsumedPartnerCycle` (partner has not completed a NEW cycle since this route last consumed one).
- **Alternation state: new sparse scalar `Route.LastConsumedPartnerCycle`** (default **0**, NOT -1 - a fresh mutual chain has both routes at 0 with the partner at 0 completions, so both compute `0 <= 0` = held, the deadlock the seed rule breaks; -1 would let both dispatch on cycle 0). Advanced on a genuine dispatch (`RouteOrchestrator.AdvancePartnerAlternationOnDispatch`, gated on `LinkedRouteId != null`) to `partner.CompletedCycles`, so the route holds until the partner completes ANOTHER cycle. Set at the dispatch-emit site in BOTH firing paths: single-stop `ProcessLoopRoute` only when `emitted == true` (NOT on the ELS-replay backstop, which would skip a partner cycle), and multi-stop `ProcessMultiStopCrossings` inside the `!dispatchAlready` first-commit branch (a dispatchAlready resume does NOT re-advance). Codec: sparse omit-at-0 (mirrors `dispatchPriority` / `lastObservedLoopCycleIndex`), so an unlinked / pre-M4c route writes NOTHING new and round-trips byte-identically. NOT reset on Activate / cadence-rebase (it is chain state, not per-cycle fire state - resetting it would break alternation across a pause/resume).
- **Bypass when the partner is missing / Paused / Broken** (design 10.14). The bypass set is precisely `!RouteStatusPolicy.GhostDriving(partner.Status)` (Paused + EndpointLost + MissingSourceRecording + SourceChanged) PLUS an unresolved partner (`TryGetRoute` false): exactly the partners that will never advance `CompletedCycles`, so holding on them would stall the route forever. Bypassed -> the route dispatches on its own schedule.
- **Deadlock seed (mutual A<->B link, neither completed).** The SEED (the route that sorts first by `IsChainSeed` - lower `DispatchPriority`, then ordinal `Id`; mirrors `CompareRoutesForTick`'s first + last keys but OMITS the schedule-state `NextDispatchUT` middle key so the seed is a STABLE structural property of the pair) treats the constraint as satisfied. SCOPED to `route.CompletedCycles == 0 && partner.CompletedCycles == 0` so the bypass fires exactly ONCE - the seed's very first cycle; after the seed completes once (`CompletedCycles -> 1`) it falls to the normal alternation gate and holds until the partner completes a cycle (the `route.CompletedCycles == 0` clause is load-bearing: without it the seed would re-dispatch every cycle while the partner stayed at 0, starving the partner).
- **M6 hold reason.** `LogisticsHoldPresentation.DescribeHold` gains a `WaitingForPartner` case rendering "waiting for the linked route '{partnerName}' to complete its run" (generic clause when the `partner:` token is missing). Routed through the existing hold-reason surface: the loop-blocked branch's `RecordHold(elig.Kind, elig.Reason, ...)` persists the kind + the `partner:<name>` token; the route stays GhostDriving while waiting, and `ShouldDisplayHold` shows the hold on the Active row.
- **Logging.** The partner gate emits a Verbose audit line per crossing for its HOLD / SEED / BYPASS / CLEAR decision (partner name, `partner.CompletedCycles` vs `LastConsumedPartnerCycle`); the advance emits a Verbose `consumed partner cycle K -> K+1` line. One documented exception to the evaluator's "no logging" contract (the gate runs once per crossing, not per frame, and the seed/bypass branches are otherwise invisible to the orchestrator since they return an ELIGIBLE result).
- **Tests (xUnit).** New `RouteRoundTripLinkTests` (drives the REAL `ProcessLoopRoute` path via `Tick` + loop-unit / delivery-row seams, the `RouteMultiStopFireTests` pattern, plus evaluator-level `CheckEligibility` / `PartnerConstraintSatisfied` checks): strict A->B->A alternation (full Tick); B holds until the partner completes a NEW cycle (evaluator-level, isolated from same-tick order); blocked partner -> B holds WaitingForPartner naming A (full Tick); Paused partner + missing partner bypass + dispatch on own schedule; deadlock mutual link -> seed eligible / non-seed waits, then alternates; seed bypass is one-shot (seed holds after its first cycle); unlinked route gate-skipped + byte-behaviour-identical (no PartnerGate log); gate ORDERED LAST (a cargo-short linked route surfaces OriginLacksCargo, not WaitingForPartner); the bypass set matches `!GhostDriving` over all 9 statuses (Theory by name). `RouteCodecTests.RoundTrip_LastConsumedPartnerCycle_SparseDefaultZero` (sparse omit-at-0 + byte-identity for unlinked + non-zero round-trip). `LogisticsHoldPresentationTests` (WaitingForPartner names the partner / generic clause / shows on Active / ASCII guard). `RouteFixtureBuilder.WithLastConsumedPartnerCycle` added. `dotnet test` green.

### Logistics M4c Phase C2 - in-game validation + M4c docs close + M4 COMPLETE (done, branch `logistics-m4-multistop`)

Plan `docs/dev/plan-logistics-m4-shape-generality.md` Phase C2: closes M4c (and all of M4) end-to-end with in-game tests + the user-facing CHANGELOG line + the design-doc flips. NO production-code change (the C1 chain-constraint scheduler is complete); this phase is in-game tests + docs only. With round-trip done, **M4 (shape generality - multi-stop + multi-origin + round-trip) is COMPLETE.**

- **In-game `LogisticsRoundTripRuntimeTests`** (new `Source/Parsek/InGameTests/`, `[InGameTest(Category="Logistics", Scene=FLIGHT, AllowBatchExecution=false, RestoreBatchFlightBaselineAfterExecution=true)]`, isolated-batch + `WaitForActiveVesselUnpack` discipline). Four tests; live validation (Ctrl+Shift+T) is the maintainer's playtest, the M1/M2/M3/M4a/M4b pattern. Both routes are harvest-origin single-stop DELIVERY routes (no KSC funds / origin debit - isolates the chain constraint from machinery already covered by M1/M2/M3/M4b) crediting a tiny LiquidFuel amount onto the LIVE active vessel through the production `Tick` -> `ProcessLoopRoute` -> `EmitLoopCycle` -> `ApplyDelivery` path; the live endpoint is snapshotted + restored in finally. (1) `RoundTrip_StaggeredDocks_AlternatesAcrossTicks` (5.4, the headline + the C1-review coverage nit): two linked routes A (dock phase 1300) and B (dock phase 1700) with DIFFERENT recorded dock phases so the REAL CROSS-TICK alternation runs, NOT a same-tick co-dispatch artifact. Tick 1 (UT 1300) reaches ONLY A's dock -> A (seed) completes its cycle while B is not due AND would hold WaitingForPartner naming A (asserted evaluator-level for order-independence); tick 2 (UT 1700) reaches B's dock -> B becomes eligible (A completed) + dispatches + consumes A's cycle (cursor -> 1) while A does NOT re-fire. At most one of the pair advances per tick (the "one transport's worth of effects" guarantee, design 5.4), asserted via `CompletedCycles` progression + the `WaitingForPartner` hold. (2) `RoundTrip_PausedPartner_BypassesAndDispatches` (10.14): B linked to a PAUSED partner A (B has consumed A's baseline so the alternation gate WOULD hold it) dispatches on its OWN schedule via the non-ghost-driving bypass; A dispatches nothing. (3) `RoundTrip_DeadlockSeed_SeedDispatchesFirst`: a fresh mutual A<->B link (both docks at 1300) - `IsChainSeed` deterministic (A is seed by priority); evaluator-level the SEED is eligible (deadlock break) + the non-seed HOLDS WaitingForPartner; the Tick completes the seed (then the non-seed alternates in within-tick once the seed completed). (4) `RoundTrip_SaveReload_PreservesAlternation`: a linked pair (A completed 1, B consumed it -> B holds WaitingForPartner) survives a real `GamePersistence.SaveGame` (B's `lastConsumedPartnerCycle=1` WRITTEN, A's omitted at the 0 default - sparse byte-identity), reloads via the production `RouteStore.LoadRoutesFrom` codec with the cursor intact, still holds, and becomes eligible again only after the partner completes ANOTHER cycle (alternation resumes from the persisted cursor). Pauses time warp across the save; deletes the disposable slot in finally. A precondition that can't be met (null active vessel, save layout mismatch) calls `InGameAssert.Skip` with a named reason - never a hard fail.
- **No synthetic recording added.** The round-trip cases drive the alternation via the loop-unit resolver seam + committed backing trees (the ERS membership gate), so no new `InjectAllRecordings` fixture is needed (the M4a multi-stop + M4b multi-origin synthetics already exercise the firing path).
- **CHANGELOG.** One `## Unreleased` Features line scoped PRECISELY to round-trip linking: two one-way routes can be linked as a round-trip pair so they alternate (one dispatches only after its partner completes a run), modeling a single reused transport (outbound + return); a paused partner is bypassed. Does NOT overclaim M5 (inter-body re-aim) or M6.
- **Design-doc flips.** 19.4 M4 round-trip bullet -> SHIPPED (M4c) with the as-built note (the thin `LinkedRouteId` chain-constraint via the `WaitingForPartner` eligibility hold - NOT a new RouteStatus; `LastConsumedPartnerCycle` alternation cursor; bypass a Paused/Broken/missing partner; lower-priority/id deadlock seed; the M6 "waiting for partner" hold reason) + the **M4 COMPLETE** note (multi-stop + multi-origin + round-trip all SHIPPED). Section 9 (Round-Trip Linking) flipped from "(Future)" to SHIPPED (M4c). Section 10.14 (linked partner paused) flipped from "(future)" to SHIPPED (M4c). Missions locked-layer git diff stays EMPTY. NO M5/M6 overclaim (those stay future).
- **Verification.** `dotnet test` green at 15992 (C2 is tests-via-`InGameTest` + docs, so no xUnit count change). The Parsek project compiles (the in-game tests build via the Tests-project ProjectReference). LIVE validation (Ctrl+Shift+T) PENDING - the maintainer's playtest.

### Logistics M4 PR #1180 adversarial-review fixes (done, branch `logistics-m4-multistop`)

A 2-agent adversarial review of the full PR #1180 (M4a/b/c + link UI + both static-handler data-loss fixes) reported HIGH confidence with no blockers. Findings + resolutions:

- ~~**MAJOR - multi-origin cargo escrow STRANDS on a mid-cycle quiesce.**~~ FIXED. `DropRouteEscrow` ran only at multi-stop cycle-complete + `RemoveRoute` + scene-switch/main-menu `ClearAllEscrow`; a route that left ghost-driving MID-cycle (player **Pause**, `RevalidateSources` into `MissingSourceRecording`/`SourceChanged`, or **EndpointLost** at dispatch or delivery) never reached the cycle-complete sweep, so its dispatch-time reservation stranded and `OtherRoutesReservedFor` kept mis-gating a competing route sharing that source (wrong, persistent `WaitingForResources` hold with a misleading "source out of X" reason) until the next scene switch. Fix: an idempotent `RouteStore.DropRouteEscrow(route.Id)` at every quiesce transition (six sites) - `RouteOrchestrator.TryPause` immediate-pause branch, `RouteStore.RevalidateSources` into-source-problem edge, `ApplyEndpointLost`, the delivery-time `endpoint-lost-at-delivery` transition, and (added after a clean follow-up review caught the gap) the `delivered-then-paused` transition in `ApplyDeliveryFromPlan` (a Send-Once-armed multi-stop route pausing mid-PARTIAL-cycle, which never reaches the cycle-complete sweep). Tested by `RouteCargoEscrowTests.TryPause_MidCycle_DropsHeldEscrow_SoCompetingRouteNotMisGated` (+ the clean-no-op companion).
- ~~**MINOR - single-stop escrow path had no cycle-complete drop safety net.**~~ FIXED. The multi-stop path sweeps residual escrow at cycle-complete (the C2 reserve-pid != release-pid divergence guard); the single-stop `EmitLoopCycle` had neither the sweep nor a test. Added the same idempotent `DropRouteEscrow(route.Id)` at the end of `EmitLoopCycle`'s emitted-true path, mirroring `ProcessMultiStopCrossings`. No-op on the normal leak-free path (reserve == release netted to zero).
- ~~**NIT - the GameEvent-handler contract test was a hardcoded `[InlineData]` allowlist.**~~ FIXED. A forgotten future entry would miss the next static handler (the exact wipe class). `ScenarioGameEventHandlerContractTests` now SOURCE-SCANS `ParsekScenario.cs` for every `GameEvents.*.Add(/Remove(` subscription and asserts each resolved handler is non-static (auto-covers future subscriptions); the known-6 `[Theory]` stays as belt-and-suspenders.
- ~~**NIT - round-trip same-tick simultaneous dispatch.**~~ DOCUMENTED (intended). If both linked routes' dock phases land in one tick the seed advances first and the partner then un-gates within the same tick, so they both fire (rather than alternate). Consistent with the accepted one-cycle cold-start overlap and asserted as intended by `RoundTrip_StaggeredDocks` (distinct phases => clean alternation). Design §9 now documents it; strict same-tick alternation would need a tick-start `CompletedCycles` snapshot.
- **MINOR (NO code change - PLAYTEST PENDING) - `OnMainMenuTransition` reactivation.** Making the handler instance re-activated its per-scene-switch `FlushStalePendingRecoveryFunds` + `RecoveryPayoutContextStore.Clear` (dormant ~3 months; `FlushStale...` clears the WHOLE pending queue). Both review lenses could NOT construct a corruption case; the existing rationale comment argues a recovery can't pair across a scene boundary. Changing the scope blind risks a ledger regression, so the resolution is the standing playtest (recover a vessel -> immediately switch scene -> confirm funds credited + no spurious eviction Warn), shared with the `OnMainMenuTransition` known-bug entry above. A reactivation note was added at the call site; if a legit recovery is ever evicted, scope the flush to MAINMENU.
- **Verification.** Full xUnit suite green (see the commit). Escrow drops are idempotent no-ops on the leak-free path, so single-stop / delivery-only / non-quiescing routes are behaviorally unchanged.

### Logistics M3 Phase 1 - analysis: pickup classification + flow closure (resources) (done, branch `logistics-m3-direction`)

Plan `docs/dev/plan-logistics-m3-direction-generality.md` Phase 1 (analysis only; route-shape codec / reverse writer / two-direction applier / inventory pickup are Phases 2-5, all DONE - see their sections below). Design doc 19.4 M3 bullet 4 carries the as-built note. Phase 7 (in-game validation) is DONE - all 5 LogisticsPickupRuntimeTests passed live (see the consolidated Phase 7 section below).

- **Resource pickup now classifies, no longer rejects (D2).** `RouteAnalysisEngine.BuildResourceLoadManifest` is the sign-flip mirror of the delivery builder (`loaded = min(endpointLoss, transportGain)`, undefined names excluded on the admission direction; `HasResourcePickup` stays the rejection-direction presence detector that keeps seeing undefined names). A pure-pickup or mixed deliver-and-pickup window is now Eligible with `RouteAnalysisResult.ResourceLoadManifest` set. The note above ("Drilling while docked at the DESTINATION still rejects `MixedPickupDelivery`") is SUPERSEDED for the resource case by Phase 1: resource pickup admits. ~~**Still rejecting `MixedPickupDelivery` (value 4, unchanged):** an INVENTORY (stored-part) pickup - lifted in Phase 5.~~ DONE in Phase 5: inventory pickup admits too; `MixedPickupDelivery` now fires only for an UNWITNESSED inventory gain (a transport stored-part gain the endpoint did not give it), the non-fungible window-local closure.
- **Flow closure (D3).** `ComputeFlowClosure` (presence-gated on complete run manifests per OQ2) rejects the new `RouteAnalysisStatus.FlowDoesNotClose` (value 8) only on over-delivery (pre-clamp slack `< -GainEpsilon`: more left aboard than `launched + loaded + harvested - delivered`, with `residual = window.UndockTransportResources`). Positive slack is legitimate consumption and never rejects. Closure sums over a window LIST (length 1 in M3a) so M4 multi-window is a fill-in. In M3a single-window, an over-delivery that the M2 gain check (dock-time) misses but closure catches is a phantom post-window transport gain (the over-delivery xUnit fixtures pin this).
- **Gate fixes (D4).** `NoDeliveryManifest` widened to "no delivery AND no load" so a pure-pickup window reaches Eligible; the M2 harvest gain check threads the window's loaded term as a witnessed source so a pickup does not false-reject `UntrackedCargoGain` (the loaded-term composition is M4-ready - in M3a single-window it is a no-op for physically consistent data since a pickup never elevates the pre-couple dock-transport baseline).
- **Surfacing:** `FlowDoesNotClose` threads a named-quantity `RejectDetail` ("Ore: 30.0 over-delivered") through `RouteCreationFormatters.FormatRejectMessage` and the `RouteCandidateFinder` near-miss batch summary exactly like `UntrackedCargoGain`. The `MixedPickupDelivery` reject copy was rewritten for its new inventory-only reachability.
- **Pending (later phases):** ~~route-shape `PickupManifest` codec (Phase 2)~~ DONE (see the Phase 2 section below); reverse resource writer re-aimed at the per-window endpoint (Phase 3), the `RouteCargoPickedUp = 29` ledger row + re-keyed replay backstop + two-direction `EmitLoopCycle` applier (Phase 4, the pickup-only reload-idempotency hole), inventory pickup (Phase 5), in-game `LogisticsPickupRuntimeTests` (Phase 7).

### Logistics M3 Phase 2 - route shape + codec (done, branch `logistics-m3-direction`)

Plan `docs/dev/plan-logistics-m3-direction-generality.md` Phase 2 (D8/D9); reverse writer / two-direction applier / inventory pickup are Phases 3-5, NOT yet built. Design doc 19.4 M3 route-shape bullet carries the Phase 2 as-built note.

- **Route-shape pickup manifests (D8).** `RouteStop` gains `PickupManifest` (`Dictionary<string,double>`) + `InventoryPickupManifest` (`List<InventoryPayloadItem>`), the exact mirror of `DeliveryManifest` / `InventoryDeliveryManifest`.
- **Sparse codec (D8/D9).** `RouteCodec` serializes them as new `PICKUP_MANIFEST` / `INVENTORY_PICKUP_MANIFEST` nodes under each `STOP`, verbatim copies of the delivery call sites: omitted when empty (the existing `SerializeFlatResourceManifest` / `SerializeInventoryItems` skip empty), empty->null on load (no lazy alloc). A pre-M3 / delivery-only route writes nothing new and round-trips byte-identically.
- **RouteBuilder populates + admits the originless pickup (D8).** `PickupManifest` is filled from the Phase-1 `analysis.ResourceLoadManifest` (defensive copy); `InventoryPickupManifest` stays null in Phase 2 (the inventory analysis term + applier are Phase 5). An originless PURE-PICKUP run (no KSC launch, no docked-origin proof, no harvest origin, a populated load manifest, no delivery) is now ADMITTED instead of rejected `endpoint-missing`: the dock endpoint becomes the display origin (`origin=pickup:pid=...`), debited later at the per-window applier (Phase 3/4), so the route's `CostManifest` stays EMPTY (mirrors harvest origin). A MIXED window with no conventional origin still rejects `endpoint-missing` (the admission is `hasResourceLoad && !hasDelivery`-gated). Existing delivery / KSC / non-KSC / harvest routes are untouched.
- **No recording-proof change (D9, CRITICAL).** NO new `RouteConnectionWindow` field and NO `RouteProofHasher` / `RouteProofCodec` / `RouteProofMetadata` change - the pickup direction is DERIVED at analysis time, so the recording proof hash stays byte-identical (pinned by `Hash_PreM3Recording_ByteStable`) and `RouteStore.RevalidateSources` does not flip a pre-M3 / pickup-carrying route to `SourceChanged`.
- **Tests:** `RouteCodecTests` (pickup round-trip + sparse omission for null/empty/zero-count + full-populated mixed stop), `RouteBuilderTests` (originless pure-pickup admission + defensive copy + mixed-no-origin still rejects + delivery-only leaves pickup null), `RouteProofHashTests.Hash_PreM3Recording_ByteStable`, `RouteStoreValidationTests.Revalidate_StopWithPickupManifest_LeavesActiveUntouched`.
- **Pending (later phases):** reverse resource writer (Phase 3), `RouteCargoPickedUp = 29` ledger row + re-keyed replay backstop + two-direction applier (Phase 4), inventory pickup (Phase 5), in-game `LogisticsPickupRuntimeTests` (Phase 7).
- ~~**Pending (Phase 4 UI obligation):** the stop summary label in `MissionRouteStructureList` / `LogisticsWindowUI` is built from `DeliveryManifest` / `InventoryDeliveryManifest` only, so a pure-pickup stop would render a "Deliver" label describing nothing.~~ DONE in Phase 4: `RouteStructureListBuilder.FormatStopLabel` is now direction-aware - a pure-pickup stop reads "Pick up (...)", a mixed stop reads "Deliver (...) / Pick up (...)", a degenerate empty stop keeps the bare "Deliver" fallback (pinned by `StructureListBuilderTests.FormatStopLabel_*`).

### Logistics M3 Phase 3 - reverse resource writer + source probe + planner refactor (done, branch `logistics-m3-direction`)

Plan `docs/dev/plan-logistics-m3-direction-generality.md` Phase 3 (D5); the two-direction `EmitLoopCycle` applier + `RouteCargoPickedUp` row + replay re-key are Phase 4 (NOT wired here), inventory pickup is Phase 5. RESOURCES ONLY (no inventory removal in this phase). Design doc 19.4 M3 reverse-writer bullet carries the as-built note.

- **Planner is now manifest-agnostic (D5).** `RouteOriginDebitPlanner.PrepareDebit` gained a `(Dictionary<string,double> requiredAmounts, IOriginCargoProbe)` overload; the existing `(Route, IOriginCargoProbe)` overload now delegates to it with `route.CostManifest` (byte-behaviour-identical, so the M1 origin-debit path is UNCHANGED). The `available = min(required, stored)` clamp, the non-positive skip, the negative-stored floor, and the ordinal ordering are shared by both, so the SAME planner now serves the M1 dispatch-time origin debit and the M3 per-window PICKUP manifest.
- **Writer decoupled from the Route (D5).** `LiveOriginDebitWriters` no longer stores a `Route`; the M1 ctor `(Route, Vessel, plan, isLoaded)` delegates to a new route-agnostic ctor `(string routeIdForLog, Vessel targetVessel, plan, isLoaded)`. The route id is diagnostic only (the "Origin debit:" log line); neither the removal arithmetic (`pr.amount -= delta` loaded / `prs.amount -= delta` unloaded, clamp-at-zero, `ShouldDeliverToResource` flow gate) nor the tank-pool reads were touched, so the writer operates on a TARGET vessel + a prepared plan + the captured `isLoaded`, independent of which manifest produced the plan.
- **Reusable per-window endpoint-debit path (D5).** `RouteOrchestrator.ApplyPickupDebit(endpoint, pickupManifest, env, routeIdForLog)` is the mirror of `ApplyOriginDebit` re-aimed at the per-window pickup ENDPOINT: it resolves the endpoint vessel via `env.TryResolveEndpointVessel` (production `RouteEndpointResolver`), captures the loaded gate ONCE for THAT vessel (per-vessel, never hoisted), builds `LiveOriginCargoProbe`, plans via the manifest overload, applies via `LiveOriginDebitWriters`, and returns an `OriginDebitOutcome` (here `OriginVesselPid` carries the ENDPOINT pid). An empty/null manifest is a structural no-op (resolved, zero actuals, not short); an unresolved-or-resolved-null endpoint is honest unresolved bookkeeping (Warn, zero actuals, FULL requested manifest, short) exactly like the origin path; a short source clamps to stored and records the full requested amount on `RequestedOnShortfall`. A `PickupDebitApplierForTesting` seam mirrors `OriginDebitApplierForTesting` for the Phase 4 applier tests.
- **Not wired + no ledger row (Phase 4 boundary).** `ApplyPickupDebit` is NOT called from `EmitLoopCycle` / `ProcessLoopRoute` and emits NO ledger row - the `RouteCargoPickedUp = 29` row + the direction-agnostic `(RouteId, RouteCycleId)` replay re-key (the pickup-only reload-idempotency hole) are Phase 4. Loop-path-only in spirit (M1 D11 parity); reversible via the rewind quicksave + ELS replay keys when Phase 4 wires it in.
- **Tests:** `RouteOriginDebitPlannerTests` (manifest overload clamp/short/order, non-positive skip, the M1 Route overload delegating byte-identically); `RoutePickupDebitTests` (the test seam short-circuit, empty-manifest no-op, unresolved + resolved-null-vessel honest bookkeeping, planner-level flow-gate symmetry); in-game `LogisticsPickupRuntimeTests` (live loaded + unloaded-proto endpoint removal through the production probe + writer, short clamp). The M1 origin-debit xUnit + in-game suites stay green UNCHANGED.
- **Pending (later phases):** ~~`RouteCargoPickedUp = 29` ledger row + re-keyed replay backstop + two-direction `EmitLoopCycle` applier (Phase 4)~~ DONE (see the Phase 4 section below); inventory pickup writer/probe (Phase 5), mixed bidirectional applier ordering (Phase 6), in-game scenario 3/5 `LogisticsPickupRuntimeTests` (Phase 7).

### Logistics M3 Phase 4 - orchestrator two-direction applier + pickup ledger row + replay re-key (done, branch `logistics-m3-direction`)

Plan `docs/dev/plan-logistics-m3-direction-generality.md` Phase 4 (D6 / OQ4); inventory pickup is Phase 5, mixed-window net-zero ordering refinement is Phase 6. RESOURCES ONLY. This phase makes a pure-pickup route DISPATCHABLE and physically debits its endpoint. Design doc 19.4 M3 applier bullet carries the as-built note.

- **New ledger row `RouteCargoPickedUp = 29` (OQ4 / D6), fully integrated at 5 sites.** Appended after `RouteRecoveryCredited = 28` (no renumber). It carries the ACTUAL debited manifest (`RouteResourceManifest`), the requested-on-shortfall manifest (`RouteRequestedResourceManifest`), and the ENDPOINT pid (`RouteOriginVesselPid`) - the mirror of `RouteCargoDebited` minus funds (a pickup emits ZERO funds, so its codec never writes a funds line). The 5 integration sites: (a) `GameAction` enum + serialize/deserialize dispatch + a funds-less `SerializeRouteCargoPickedUp` / `DeserializeRouteCargoPickedUp` (route rows ride the existing `GameAction` codec via `Ledger`, so `ParsekScenario` OnSave/OnLoad needs no change - verified); (b) `LedgerLoadMigration.IsResourceImpactingAction` explicit `case ... -> false` (no funds; mirrors `RouteCargoDelivered`; the `IsResourceImpactingAction_Theory` forcing test extended); (c) `FundsModule` routes it as a NON-funds row exactly like `RouteDispatched` / `RouteCargoDelivered` - INTENTIONALLY no `case` (it falls through and moves no funds; a documented no-op comment marks the omission); (d) `SupersedeCommit.IsWorldStateChangingRecordingAction` explicit `case ... -> false` (a NEW type does NOT inherit the route-rows-false above; without the case it falls to `return true` and supersede strict-blocks; the `RetryBlockingRecordingActionCases` forcing theory extended to `(false, false)`); (e) `RouteModule.ProcessCargoPickedUp` observe-only (mirror of `ProcessCargoDebited` - reads `RouteOriginVesselPid`, bumps a `PhysicalPickups` diagnostic counter, mutates nothing; T-ROUTEMODULE-OBSERVE).
- **Two-direction `EmitLoopCycle` applier (D6).** At a confirmed dock crossing the loop applier now fires, under ONE `cycleId`: the dispatch-debit half (`EmitDispatchDebit`, `RouteDispatched` Seq0 + `RouteCargoDebited` Seq1) -> the pickup half (when the stop carries a `PickupManifest`: `EmitPickupHalf` resolves the endpoint, calls the Phase 3 `ApplyPickupDebit` under the same cycleId, and emits ONE `RouteCargoPickedUp` row at Seq2, after dispatch) -> the delivery half (when the stop carries a delivery manifest). The pickup half uses the `PickupDebitApplierForTesting` seam.
- **Pure-pickup SKIPS the delivery half (D6).** A route with no delivery manifest no longer calls `ApplyDelivery` / emits no `RouteCargoDelivered` row (previously `EmitLoopCycle` ALWAYS called `ApplyDelivery`, emitting a delivered row even on an empty plan). The delivery half is gated on `RouteHasDeliveryManifest`; the pure-pickup branch bumps `CompletedCycles` itself (the analogue of `ApplyDelivery`'s bump) so the cycleId advances.
- **Replay backstop RE-KEY (OQ4, the correctness fix).** The per-cycle ELS idempotency guard in `EmitLoopCycle` was keyed on the `RouteCargoDelivered` row (`IsDeliveryAlreadyInLedger`), which a pickup-only route never emits -> the endpoint debit re-applied every save/reload. It is now keyed on the DIRECTION-AGNOSTIC `RouteDispatched` row (`IsDispatchAlreadyInLedger`, every cycle emits exactly one) over `(RouteId, RouteCycleId)`, preserving the existing `CompletedCycles` bump on the replay branch (or a pickup-only route replay-skips forever). LOOP-PATH-ONLY: the legacy `ApplyDelivery`-path `IsDeliveryAlreadyInLedger` call stays on `RouteCargoDelivered` (dead for loop routes, M1 D11).
- **Direction-aware stop label (the Phase-2 deferred UI obligation).** `RouteStructureListBuilder.FormatStopLabel` renders "Pick up (...)" for a pure-pickup stop, "Deliver (...) / Pick up (...)" for a mixed stop, and the bare "Deliver" fallback for a degenerate stop.
- **Tests:** `RouteLoopPickupFireTests` (mixed window fires both halves under one cycleId; pickup row Sequence after dispatch; pure-pickup emits NO delivered row; delivery-only unchanged with no pickup row; **the headline `PurePickup_ReplayedCycle_IsIdempotent_NoSecondDebit`** - a re-presented pickup-only crossing emits nothing and the endpoint debit is NOT re-invoked; replay branch bumps CompletedCycles; crashed delivery disposition still debits the pickup; short-pickup records the requested manifest + warns; the `RouteHasPickupManifest` / `RouteHasDeliveryManifest` decision helpers); `GameActionSerializationTests.Serialize_RouteCargoPickedUp_RoundTripsManifestsAndEndpointPid_NoFunds`; `RouteModuleTests.ProcessCargoPickedUp_*` (observe-only, pid-0 not physical); `LegacyTreeMigrationTests.IsResourceImpactingAction_Theory` (+ pickup false); `SupersedeCommitTests` (pickup `(false, false)` + the `RouteCargoPickedUp_ExcludedFromWorldStateChangingPredicate` assertion); `StructureListBuilderTests.FormatStopLabel_*`; the existing loop replay tests re-seeded onto `RouteDispatched`.
- **Pending (later phases):** ~~inventory pickup writer/probe (Phase 5)~~ DONE (see the Phase 5 section below); ~~mixed bidirectional applier ordering for net-zero same-resource flows (Phase 6)~~ DONE (see the Phase 6 section below); in-game scenario 3/5 `LogisticsPickupRuntimeTests` (Phase 7).

### Logistics M3 Phase 5 - inventory pickup (window-local) + carve-out lift (done, branch `logistics-m3-direction`)

Plan `docs/dev/plan-logistics-m3-direction-generality.md` Phase 5 (D7 / OQ3); mixed-window net-zero ordering refinement is Phase 6, in-game scenario 3/5 sweep is Phase 7. This phase makes inventory (stored-part) pickup work end to end, WINDOW-LOCAL (no full-run `Start/EndTransportInventory` fields). Design doc 19.4 M3 bullet 5 carries the as-built note.

- **Analysis: classify, do not reject (D7).** `RouteAnalysisEngine.BuildInventoryLoadManifest` is the sign-flip mirror of `BuildInventoryDeliveryManifest` (per exact `InventoryPayloadItem.IdentityHash`, `loaded = min(endpointLoss, transportGain)`, identity carried intact, the source-side `DockEndpointInventory` STOREDPART as the canonical copy). `HasUnwitnessedInventoryGain` is the non-fungible WINDOW-LOCAL closure: a transport inventory GAIN with NO matching endpoint LOSS fails closed (inventory has no harvested provenance). `MixedPickupDelivery` (value 4, unchanged) now fires ONLY for that unwitnessed gain - a clean inventory pickup classifies into the new `RouteAnalysisResult.InventoryLoadManifest` and ADMITS. `HasInventoryPickup` is retained as a directly-tested presence detector (dead in the eligibility flow, like `HasResourcePickup`).
- **Route shape (D8).** `RouteBuilder` populates `RouteStop.InventoryPickupManifest` from `analysis.InventoryLoadManifest` (deep copy; Phase 2 left it null). The originless pure-pickup admission now fires on `hasLoad = hasResourceLoad || hasInventoryLoad` (a pure-INVENTORY pickup admits with `origin=pickup:pid=...` and empty cost manifests, same as the pure-resource pickup).
- **Source probe + REMOVE writer (the only genuinely new mutation, D7).** `LiveInventoryPickupWriter` LOCATES a stored item by `IdentityHash` and REMOVES it: loaded - walk `ModuleInventoryPart.storedParts`, hash each slot's `StoredPart` via `StoredPart.Save` -> `VesselSpawner.ComputeInventoryPayloadIdentityHash`, take the LOWEST slot index (deterministic partial-match), clear via stock `ClearPartAtSlot`; unloaded - walk the proto `STOREDPARTS` nodes, hash each, remove the matching node. The transport credit is bookkeeping only (no physical transport write - the transport never materializes). Identity stability is the contract: the `StoredPart.Save` shape equals the recorded depot snapshot shape after the canonical slotIndex/quantity strip, and vessel-local transients (cid/persistentId/position/temp/...) are stripped, so the live source slot matches the recorded depot payload cross-vessel and proto-vs-loaded.
- **Applier + ledger row (D7).** `RouteOrchestrator.ApplyInventoryPickupDebit` (sibling of `ApplyPickupDebit`, its own `InventoryPickupApplierForTesting` seam, `InventoryPickupOutcome` return) is wired into `EmitPickupHalf` alongside the resource pickup under one `cycleId`. The `RouteCargoPickedUp` row gains sparse `ROUTE_INVENTORY_MANIFEST` / `ROUTE_REQUESTED_INVENTORY_MANIFEST` codec nodes carrying the picked-up stored-part payloads (the FIRST ledger-row inventory manifest; delivery inventory is applied physically, never on the row) - omitted when empty so a resource-only pickup row stays byte-identical. The `GameAction.RouteInventoryManifest` / `RouteRequestedInventoryManifest` fields are `internal` (not `public`) because `InventoryPayloadItem` is an internal type. Idempotency rides the Phase-4 dispatch-keyed replay backstop unchanged.
- **Carve-out LIFTED (D7).** The M1 `inventory-origin-debit-unsupported` HOLD (`LiveRouteRuntimeEnvironment.OriginHasCargo` + `RouteOriginCargoCheck.RequiresInventoryDebit`) is REMOVED. The same `LiveInventoryPickupWriter` now serves the origin-dispatch inventory debit: `ApplyOriginDebit` removes `route.InventoryCostManifest` items by identity and the `RouteCargoDebited` row carries them via the same sparse codec; the gate is all-or-nothing via the new `RouteOriginCargoCheck.HasRequiredInventory` (`LiveInventoryPickupWriter.CountStored` by identity, same per-vessel loaded-gate capture as the resource gate). A short origin holds with an `inventory:<hash>` short token, which `LogisticsHoldPresentation.DescribeHold` renders as "origin is missing a required stored part". The decision was to LIFT (preferred-if-clean) because the writer is a vessel-agnostic identity-based reuse serving both the per-window pickup AND the origin-dispatch path.
- **Tests:** `RouteInventoryPickupTests` (BuildInventoryLoadManifest sign-flip + min-clamp + delivery-direction-returns-null; HasUnwitnessedInventoryGain true/false/partial; **cross-vessel + proto-vs-loaded identity hash stability**; HasRequiredInventory short/covered/empty; ApplyInventoryPickupDebit seam/empty/unresolved/resolved-null; **deterministic lowest-slot partial-match** via `FindUnloadedMatchNode`); `RouteAnalysisEngineTests` (inventory pickup flips reject -> admit; unwitnessed gain rejects window-local + diagnostic names identity - the Phase-1 "inventory still rejects" tests updated); `RouteBuilderTests` (originless inventory pickup admits + InventoryPickupManifest deep copy); `GameActionSerializationTests` (RouteCargoPickedUp inventory manifest round-trip + sparse omission); `RouteLoopPickupFireTests.InventoryPickup_FiresInventoryHalf_RowCarriesInventoryManifest`; `RouteCreationFormattersTests` / `LogisticsHoldPresentationTests` (the MixedPickupDelivery + inventory-hold copy updated). In-game `LogisticsPickupRuntimeTests` adds loaded inventory removal (live ClearPartAtSlot, restored) + identity-not-held clamp-short cases (compile-only here; needs live KSP).
- **Pending (later phases):** ~~mixed bidirectional applier ordering for net-zero same-resource flows (Phase 6)~~ DONE (see the Phase 6 section below); in-game scenario 3/5 `LogisticsPickupRuntimeTests` (Phase 7).

### Logistics M3 Phase 6 - mixed bidirectional window applier ordering (done, branch `logistics-m3-direction`)

Plan `docs/dev/plan-logistics-m3-direction-generality.md` Phase 6 (D6 / D3); in-game scenario 3/5 sweep is Phase 7. This phase HARDENS the mixed-window applier ordering rule for net-zero / partially-overlapping same-resource flows. **No behavior delta:** the audit found the Phase-4/5 applier ALREADY fires the two physical halves in the correct order (pickup-debit before delivery-credit), so Phase 6 is an explicit-ordering hardening (comment + regression tests), NOT a code rewrite - hence no CHANGELOG line (CHANGELOG-style rule: user-facing behavior changes only). Design doc 19.4 M3 mixed-window bullet carries the as-built note.

- **Audit: the current order is pickup-debit BEFORE delivery-credit, and it is correct.** `EmitLoopCycle` fires, under one `cycleId`: dispatch-debit half -> pickup half (`EmitPickupHalf` -> `ApplyPickupDebit`, physically DEBITS the endpoint's source tank => FREES space) -> delivery half (`ApplyDelivery`, physically CREDITS the endpoint's destination tank => FILLS it). Both halves resolve the SAME `stop.Endpoint` => the SAME physical vessel, so for a resource both delivered AND picked up at one dock the two writes hit the SAME tank and ORDER decides the result. The shipped order is replay-deterministic: a fixed statement order inside `EmitLoopCycle`, idempotent across re-presentation via the Phase-4 dispatch-keyed backstop (the whole cycle never re-runs either half).
- **The ordering rule, now EXPLICIT (D6/D3 - the phantom-clamp invariant).** Endpoint DEBIT (pickup) MUST precede endpoint CREDIT (delivery): the debit frees capacity first, so `ApplyDelivery`'s live `LiveDeliveryCapacityProbe` + `LiveDeliveryWriters.WriteResourceLoaded` (which read LIVE tank state AFTER the debit and clamp the fill at `free = pr.maxAmount - pr.amount`) see MAXIMUM free space. A same-resource deliver+pickup nets correctly with NO phantom clamp. The WRONG order (delivery-then-pickup) would clamp a delivery into a near-full endpoint at `maxAmount`, silently WASTE the surplus, then debit from the post-clamp state - a different, lossy result than the witnessed recording. Pinned with a load-bearing comment block in `EmitLoopCycle` at both the pickup-half and delivery-half sites.
- **Inventory dimension (D7).** Inventory pickup (the inventory half of `EmitPickupHalf`, removes STOREDPART slots by `IdentityHash`) and inventory delivery (`ApplyDelivery`'s inventory writer, stores STOREDPART slots) act on different identity / resource spaces than resource tanks, so they rarely collide on one tank; the same debit-before-credit order still holds and is harmless when they do not overlap. Stated in the comment.
- **Flow closure already handles both terms for a mixed window (D3).** `ComputeFlowClosure` takes `loadedWindows` and `deliveredWindows` as LISTS and sums per-resource-name, so the SAME resource appearing in both lists for one window is balanced correctly (`slack = launched + Sum(loaded) + harvested - Sum(delivered) - residual`). The pickup raises the arrived side so an elevated residual (run kept the picked-up cargo aboard) is fully accounted - no phantom over-delivery on a balanced mixed window.
- **Tests (pin the rule as a regression guard):** `RouteLoopPickupFireTests.MixedSameResourceWindow_PickupFiresBeforeDelivery` (records the invocation order of both physical halves via the seams on an Ore-deliver + Ore-pickup window; asserts pickup strictly precedes delivery, the load-bearing order); `RouteAnalysisEngineTests.ComputeFlowClosure_MixedSameResourceWindow_BothTermsBalance` (balanced same-resource mixed window closes) + `ComputeFlowClosure_MixedSameResourceWindow_OverDelivery_Rejects` (an uncovered same-resource mixed over-delivery still rejects `FlowDoesNotClose` naming the quantity). The existing `MixedWindow_FiresPickupAndDelivery_UnderOneCycleId` / `MixedWindow_ReplayedCycle_IsIdempotent_NoSecondFire` continue to cover one-cycleId firing + replay idempotency.
- **Pending (Phase 7):** the in-game `LogisticsPickupRuntimeTests` must be RUN in a live KSP flight scene before the M3a PR merges - see the consolidated Phase 7 note below.

### Logistics M3 Phase 7 - in-game validation (DONE - all 5 validated live 2026-06-15, branch `logistics-m3-direction`)

Phases 1-6 are all built, committed, and green in xUnit; the live-KSP debit/removal paths cannot run headless. The `LogisticsPickupRuntimeTests` (`Source/Parsek/InGameTests/LogisticsPickupRuntimeTests.cs`) were RUN live (logs `2026-06-15_2048_m3-pickup-ingame-4`, 0 Parsek errors) and all five PASSED with mutation evidence in the KSP.log. (The four loaded-path tests initially precondition-skipped 3x because the isolated-batch baseline restore reloads FLIGHT and leaves the active vessel packed; fixed in commit `c45a4e836` by yielding for unpack via `LogisticsOriginDebitRuntimeTests.WaitForActiveVesselUnpack` before the precondition, converting the 3 `void` tests to `IEnumerator`.) The five validated paths:

1. **Live resource endpoint debit - loaded** (`PickupDebit_LoadedEndpointVessel_RemovesManifestAmount`): `ApplyPickupDebit` re-aimed at the loaded active vessel removes the manifest LiquidFuel through the live `PartResource.amount` writer, outcome carries the actual-debited manifest + endpoint pid, not short.
2. **Live resource endpoint debit - unloaded** (`PickupDebit_UnloadedEndpointVessel_WritesProtoSnapshot`): the same against an existing on-rails (unloaded) vessel from the save drains `ProtoPartResourceSnapshot.amount` through the unloaded writer (skips with a named reason when no debitable unloaded vessel exists).
3. **Live resource endpoint debit - short** (`PickupDebit_ShortEndpoint_ClampsAndRecordsRequested`): a manifest above the endpoint's stored amount clamps the removal to what is stored, marks the outcome short, and records the full requested amount on `RequestedOnShortfall`.
4. **Live inventory removal + identity match + stacked decrement** (`InventoryPickupDebit_LoadedEndpointVessel_RemovesStoredPart`): `ApplyInventoryPickupDebit` removes a witnessed stored part by `IdentityHash` via the production `LiveInventoryPickupWriter` (stock `ClearPartAtSlot`), the picked-up identity matches the witnessed one, the source stored count for that identity drops by exactly one (the stacked-decrement check), and the cargo is restored in `finally`. This also exercises the `StoredPart.Save` -> `ComputeInventoryPayloadIdentityHash` equality against the recorded depot hash - the live slot must match the recorded payload cross-vessel / proto-vs-loaded for the removal to find it.
5. **Inventory identity not held clamps short** (`InventoryPickupDebit_IdentityNotHeld_ClampsShortNoMutation`): a payload the endpoint cannot hold removes nothing, marks the outcome short, records the full witnessed quantity on `RequestedOnShortfall`, and mutates nothing (no restore needed).

Live evidence (KSP.log): loaded resource debit `LiquidFuel 4015.39->4010.39 path=loaded`; short clamp `requested 5015, actual 4015, short`; unloaded proto drain `Depot 639.72->634.72 path=unloaded`; loaded inventory `evaScienceKit count 1->0` (live `ClearPartAtSlot` + `IdentityHash` match); identity-not-held `no mutation, clamp short`. Scenario-level full playtests (scenario 5 load-at-depot/fly-home/recover; scenario 3 shuttle loaded mid-run) remain an OPTIONAL confidence pass, but the code paths they exercise are proven by the five live tests above. The M3a PR (#1160) pre-merge validation hold is CLEARED; the PR is out of draft.

### Explicitly out of scope (faithful replay is the accepted, UI-surfaced behavior; revisit only on playtest demand)

- **Gravity-assist / multi-heliocentric-leg transfers** - `ReaimClassifier` rejects more than one heliocentric leg (ReaimClassifier.cs:141-146); re-aiming a chained assist is a different problem class (the assist geometry constrains every leg jointly).
- **Atmo-direct / aerocapture arrival alignment** - no captured destination orbit means no boundary to insert an arrival hold at; the body-fixed entry/descent already self-anchors to the live rotation and lands at the correct geographic site on loop, so only the approach-to-entry seam misaligns.
- **Porkchop-style dv-optimal window planning** - evaluated in the 2026-05-28 survey and deliberately not needed by the congruent-window model (recorded tof + synodic spacing; M-MIS-3 adds geometry-aware tof centering, still not a porkchop grid).
- **Grand tours / multi-destination single missions** (land-on-every-body challenge flights) - joint faithful recurrence across many transited bodies is effectively never; the accepted loop behavior is faithful replay plus whatever per-leg alignment M-MIS-6/7 provide. No whole-tour alignment is planned.
- **Crew rotation / tourism as DELIVERABLES** - the mission loop renders a crew ferry fine today; counting kerbals as route cargo (crew manifests, rotation credit) is logistics-roadmap territory (`docs/parsek-logistics-supply-routes-design.md` section 19, added by PR #1113), not a Missions milestone.
- **Off-world construction launches** (Extraplanetary Launchpads-class mods: vessels rolled out from a base instead of KSC) - modded compatibility tier; revisit only on demand.

---

## Done 2026-06-12 - Logistics M2: resource generality (mod resources) + harvest provenance (branch `logistics-m2-resource-generality`)

**Milestone M2 complete** (design `docs/parsek-logistics-supply-routes-design.md` 19.4 M2 / 19.2.2 item 3 / 19.2.4; plan `docs/dev/plan-logistics-m2-resource-generality.md`). The logistics pipeline is officially resource-agnostic (any `PartResourceDefinition`-backed resource, modded included) and mining routes (scenario family 4) work end to end. Six deliverables:

- **Transferability rule, one authority:** `Logistics/ResourceTransferability.cs` (`IsRoutableResource`): not-EC/IntakeAir AND defined; undefined names excluded from ADMISSION-direction outputs only (delivery manifest / CostManifest / funds) and logged, still visible to REJECTION-direction checks (D2 direction-sensitivity - a mod uninstall can never flip a reject to Eligible); capture stays permissive; CRP-style fixtures (`Generators/CrpFixtures.cs`) threaded through the capture / analysis / delivery / origin-cargo / serialization / hash / funds suites.
- **Full-run transport-scoped cargo manifests:** new presence-gated `RouteRunCargoManifest` (pid scope at recording BIRTH, write-once start half, END half only on ACTIVE stops with `EndCaptured`, VOIDED on background transit), on every recording birth flavor (root, undock-split child, dock-merge child, chain birth; never BG-promotion / quickload resume). The legacy display-grade `StartResources`/`EndResources` were left untouched; absence of the new node is the old/new discriminator.
- **Harvest-window capture:** `RouteHarvestWindow` on `BaseConverter`-derived activity threshold crossings (covers stock harvesters/converters + asteroid/comet drills + modded derivatives, no module list), open-at-start / close-at-stop, rails-entry/exit warp re-baseline, false-alarm-resume unwind; optimizer policy (D13): splits void both halves, auto-merge refuses on windows, window-less manifests compose on scope match.
- **Analysis admission (the M2 slice of flow closure):** `RouteHarvestAnalysis.CheckTransportGains`, engaged only on complete-manifest lineages; anchor-to-dock gains must be covered by window deltas + scope-matched boundary bridges (dock seam never a bridge operand); uncovered gains reject with `RouteAnalysisStatus.UntrackedCargoGain` naming resource and quantity through the near-miss surface; the undocked-start gate refined - fully-harvest-covered undocked runs become Eligible harvest origins.
- **Harvest-origin routes + debit reduction:** `Route.IsHarvestOrigin` (display-only endpoint from the first window's open location, EMPTY CostManifest, dispatch skips origin resolution, row pair still emitted for shape stability); mixed docked-origin + harvest runs reduce the depot debit by the witnessed harvest (zero entries removed).
- **Funds basis (OQ1 decided):** the KSC per-cycle charge prices the launch manifest (`RouteRunCargoManifest.StartTransportResources` of the tree root) when the manifest is COMPLETE (same gate as the analysis, so gate and charge cannot diverge); everything else keeps the stop-snapshot walk byte-identical - existing routes keep their exact cost. Burned transit fuel is now charged; harvested cargo never is.

Plus: in-game `LogisticsHarvestRuntimeTests` (converter-toggle window lifecycle, the D5 catch-up attribution race, the D4 rails re-baseline, synthetic-tree analysis verdict) and a synthetic drill-run tree in the InjectAllRecordings set (`tree-drill-harvest-m2`). The plan went through three review rounds before coding (round 1: 3 BLOCKERs + 7 MAJORs, verdict "not sound as-is"; round 2 verification: "needs another round"; round 3 folded the corrections - the bridge-scope BLOCKER, the recording-birth discriminator, the hasher sentinel gate, the anchor backward-walk, and the narrowed optimizer merge block all came out of those rounds). Deferred scope + the manual playtest item are recorded in the open section above.

Test delta: +136 xUnit cases (15093 -> 15229, all green incl. a clean InjectAllRecordings) + 4 in-game tests.

No playback warning was observed in the session, so the impact is latent; the flat points stayed monotonic. Likely a flush-stitch bookkeeping artifact at the active<->on-rails handoff (the same session logged `AppendPointsFromTrackSections: skipped N non-monotonic frame(s) at flush stitch` #419 warnings on debris recs). ## TODO - Looped re-aim interplanetary transfer: no continuous encounter into the destination SOI; line dead-ends in open space (investigated 2026-06-15, NOT fixed - regression-sensitive, deferred)

**Symptom (playtest 2026-06-15; looped 'Duna One' mission re-aimed while flying a fresh Duna mission; log `logs/2026-06-15_1906_duna-mission-investigation`, main @a4ff95b7c V0.10.0, save s15):** the re-aimed ghost's interplanetary transfer LINE is not rendered as a proper encounter. It heads toward Duna's orbit but dead-ends in open heliocentric space, never bending into Duna's SOI; viewed mid-cruise the arc's far end sits at where Duna WILL BE at arrival (empty now), and the recorded Duna-capture hyperbola is a detached segment across a gap. The instrumented form of the same defect is a ~62 deg ghost-transform teleport at BOTH SOI handoffs (`[ReaimSeam] SEAM member=30`: Kerbin->Sun jump=87.76 Mm = 1.043x Kerbin SOI, `KSP.log:21896`; Sun->Duna jump=49.19 Mm = 1.027x Duna SOI, `KSP.log:32175`). Re-aim ENGAGED cleanly (did not decline to faithful), the Lambert solved a sane prograde transfer, and the ghost ICON does reach Duna's SOI - so the orbit is correct; the defect is the stitch / encounter rendering, not a solver failure.
